[DEBUG] Bash tool invoked with command: cat > cleanup_old_providers.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:3000/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin@agentvoiceresponse.com", "password": "agentvoiceresponse"}' \
  | jq -r '.access_token')

echo "Deleting old providers without Docker images..."

# Get all providers and delete ones with null images
curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  | jq -r '.data[] | select(.config.image == null) | .id' \
  | while read ID; do
    echo "Deleting provider: $ID"
    curl -s -X DELETE "http://localhost:3000/providers/$ID" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN"
  done

echo ""
echo "✅ Cleanup complete! Remaining providers:"
curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  | jq -r '.data[] | "- \(.name) (\(.type))"'
EOF
chmod +x cleanup_old_providers.sh && ./cleanup_old_providers.sh

#!/bin/bash
# Delete all old agents and show how to create a new one

TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:3000/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin@agentvoiceresponse.com", "password": "agentvoiceresponse"}' \
  | jq -r '.access_token')

echo "🗑️  Deleting all old agents..."
AGENTS=$(curl -s "http://localhost:3000/agents" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" | jq -r '.data[]?.id // empty')

for AGENT_ID in $AGENTS; do
  echo "  Deleting agent: $AGENT_ID"
  curl -s -X DELETE "http://localhost:3000/agents/$AGENT_ID" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN"
done

echo ""
echo "✅ All old agents deleted!"
echo ""
echo "📋 Working providers (use these for your new agent):"
echo ""

curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  | jq -r '.data[] | select(.config.image != null) | "- \(.name) (\(.type)) - ID: \(.id)"'

echo ""
echo "🎯 Now create a new agent in the dashboard:"
echo "1. Go to Agents → Create Agent"
echo "2. Name: 'My Voice Bot'"
echo "3. Mode: PIPELINE"
echo "4. Select providers:"
echo "   ASR: 'Deepgram ASR'"
echo "   LLM: 'Groq Llama 3.3 70B' or 'Cerebras Llama 3.3 70B'"
echo "   TTS: 'Edge TTS (FREE)' - the one in capitals!"
echo "5. Click Create"
echo "6. Click Run"
echo ""
echo "💡 Make sure to select the providers with Docker images!"
EOF
chmod +x /home/user/Desktop/avr-app/fix_agent.sh && /home/user/Desktop/avr-app/fix_agent.sh

[DEBUG] Bash tool invoked with command: cat > /home/user/Desktop/avr-app/delete_old_providers.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
# Delete old providers without Docker images

TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:3000/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin@agentvoiceresponse.com", "password": "agentvoiceresponse"}' \
  | jq -r '.access_token')

echo "🔍 Finding providers without Docker images..."
echo ""

# Get all providers and their details
PROVIDERS=$(curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN")

echo "Current providers:"
echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | "- \(.name) (\(.type)) - Image: \(.config.image // "null")"'
echo ""

# Get IDs of providers with null images
OLD_IDS=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.config.image == null) | .id')

if [ -z "$OLD_IDS" ]; then
  echo "✅ No broken providers found!"
else
  echo "🗑️  Deleting providers without Docker images..."
  for ID in $OLD_IDS; do
    NAME=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r ".data[] | select(.id == \"$ID\") | .name")
    echo "  Deleting: $NAME (ID: $ID)"
    RESULT=$(curl -s -X DELETE "http://localhost:3000/providers/$ID" \
      -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN")
    
    if echo "$RESULT" | grep -q "error"; then
      echo "    ❌ Failed: $(echo $RESULT | jq -r '.message')"
    else
      echo "    ✅ Deleted"
    fi
  done
fi

echo ""
echo "✅ Remaining providers (all working):"
curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  | jq -r '.data[] | "- \(.name) (\(.type))"'
EOF
chmod +x /home/user/Desktop/avr-app/delete_old_providers.sh && /home/user/Desktop/avr-app/delete_old_providers.sh

[DEBUG] Bash tool invoked with command: cat > /home/user/Desktop/avr-app/update_image_names.sh << 'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
# Update providers to use localhost/ prefixed images

TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:3000/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin@agentvoiceresponse.com", "password": "agentvoiceresponse"}' \
  | jq -r '.access_token')

echo "🔄 Updating provider image names to use localhost/ prefix..."
echo ""

# Get all providers
PROVIDERS=$(curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN")

# Update Groq
GROQ_ID=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.name == "Groq Llama 3.3 70B") | .id')
if [ ! -z "$GROQ_ID" ]; then
  echo "Updating Groq provider..."
  curl -s -X PATCH "http://localhost:3000/providers/$GROQ_ID" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{
      "config": {
        "image": "localhost/avr-llm-groq:latest",
        "env": {
          "GROQ_API_KEY": "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",
          "GROQ_MODEL": "llama-3.3-70b-versatile",
          "TEMPERATURE": "0.7",
          "MAX_TOKENS": "500"
        }
      }
    }' | jq -r '.name + " updated"'
fi

# Update Cerebras
CEREBRAS_ID=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.name == "Cerebras Llama 3.3 70B") | .id')
if [ ! -z "$CEREBRAS_ID" ]; then
  echo "Updating Cerebras provider..."
  curl -s -X PATCH "http://localhost:3000/providers/$CEREBRAS_ID" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{
      "config": {
        "image": "localhost/avr-llm-cerebras:latest",
        "env": {
          "CEREBRAS_API_KEY": "csk-45rkpchch265v85mj2e85pdtyj3pm8nmdyh85wyk82pprcc3",
          "CEREBRAS_MODEL": "llama-3.3-70b",
          "TEMPERATURE": "0.7",
          "MAX_TOKENS": "500"
        }
      }
    }' | jq -r '.name + " updated"'
fi

# Update Edge TTS
TTS_ID=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.name == "Edge TTS (FREE)") | .id')
if [ ! -z "$TTS_ID" ]; then
  echo "Updating Edge TTS provider..."
  curl -s -X PATCH "http://localhost:3000/providers/$TTS_ID" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{
      "config": {
        "image": "localhost/avr-tts-edge:latest",
        "env": {
          "VOICE": "en-US-AvaMultilingualNeural",
          "RATE": "+10%",
          "PITCH": "+2Hz"
        }
      }
    }' | jq -r '.name + " updated"'
fi

echo ""
echo "✅ All provider images updated to use localhost/ prefix!"
echo ""

# Update providers to use simple image names (no localhost prefix)

if [ ! -z "$GROQ_ID" ]; then

#!/bin/bash
# Set up local Docker registry and push custom images

set -e

echo "🐳 Setting up local Docker registry..."
echo ""

# Start local registry on port 5000
if docker ps | grep -q registry:2; then
  echo "✅ Registry already running"
else
  echo "Starting local registry on port 5000..."
  docker run -d -p 5000:5000 --name registry --restart=always registry:2
  sleep 2
  echo "✅ Registry started"
fi

echo ""
echo "🏷️  Tagging images for local registry..."

# Tag images with localhost:5000 prefix
docker tag avr-llm-groq:latest localhost:5000/avr-llm-groq:latest
docker tag avr-llm-cerebras:latest localhost:5000/avr-llm-cerebras:latest
docker tag avr-tts-edge:latest localhost:5000/avr-tts-edge:latest

echo "  ✅ Images tagged"
echo ""
echo "📤 Pushing images to local registry..."

# Push to local registry
docker push localhost:5000/avr-llm-groq:latest
docker push localhost:5000/avr-llm-cerebras:latest
docker push localhost:5000/avr-tts-edge:latest

echo ""
echo "✅ All images pushed to local registry!"

curl -s http://localhost:5000/v2/_catalog | jq

echo ""

#!/bin/bash
TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:3000/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin@agentvoiceresponse.com", "password": "agentvoiceresponse"}' \
  | jq -r '.access_token')

echo "1️⃣ Deleting ALL agents (force clean slate)..."
curl -s "http://localhost:3000/agents" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  | jq -r '.data[]?.id // empty' \
  | while read ID; do
    curl -s -X DELETE "http://localhost:3000/agents/$ID" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" > /dev/null
    echo "  ✅ Deleted agent $ID"
  done

echo ""
echo "2️⃣ Checking provider configurations..."
echo ""

PROVIDERS=$(curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN")

echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.config.image != null) | "\(.name):\n  Image: \(.config.image)\n"'

echo ""
echo "3️⃣ Checking if providers have correct localhost:5000 prefix..."

NEEDS_FIX=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.config.image != null and (.config.image | startswith("localhost:5000/") | not) and (.config.image | startswith("avr-") )) | .id')

if [ ! -z "$NEEDS_FIX" ]; then
  echo "❌ Found providers that need fixing!"
  echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.config.image != null and (.config.image | startswith("localhost:5000/") | not) and (.config.image | startswith("avr-"))) | "  - \(.name): \(.config.image)"'
  echo ""
  echo "Let me fix them..."
else
  echo "✅ All providers look good!"
fi
EOF

#!/bin/bash
# Update providers to use registry IP address

TOKEN=$(curl -s -X POST "http://localhost:3000/auth/login" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin@agentvoiceresponse.com", "password": "agentvoiceresponse"}' \
  | jq -r '.access_token')

# Get registry IP
REGISTRY_IP=$(docker network inspect avr | jq -r '.[0].Containers | to_entries[] | select(.value.Name == "registry") | .value.IPv4Address' | cut -d'/' -f1)

echo "📍 Registry IP: $REGISTRY_IP"
echo ""
echo "🔄 Updating providers to use $REGISTRY_IP:5000..."
echo ""

PROVIDERS=$(curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN")

# Update Groq
GROQ_ID=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.name == "Groq Llama 3.3 70B") | .id')
curl -s -X PATCH "http://localhost:3000/providers/$GROQ_ID" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d "{
    \"config\": {
      \"image\": \"${REGISTRY_IP}:5000/avr-llm-groq:latest\",
      \"env\": {
        \"GROQ_API_KEY\": \"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\",
        \"GROQ_MODEL\": \"llama-3.3-70b-versatile\",
        \"TEMPERATURE\": \"0.7\",
        \"MAX_TOKENS\": \"500\"
      }
    }
  }" > /dev/null
echo "✅ Groq updated to ${REGISTRY_IP}:5000/avr-llm-groq:latest"

# Update Cerebras
CEREBRAS_ID=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.name == "Cerebras Llama 3.3 70B") | .id')
curl -s -X PATCH "http://localhost:3000/providers/$CEREBRAS_ID" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d "{
    \"config\": {
      \"image\": \"${REGISTRY_IP}:5000/avr-llm-cerebras:latest\",
      \"env\": {
        \"CEREBRAS_API_KEY\": \"csk-45rkpchch265v85mj2e85pdtyj3pm8nmdyh85wyk82pprcc3\",
        \"CEREBRAS_MODEL\": \"llama-3.3-70b\",
        \"TEMPERATURE\": \"0.7\",
        \"MAX_TOKENS\": \"500\"
      }
    }
  }" > /dev/null
echo "✅ Cerebras updated to ${REGISTRY_IP}:5000/avr-llm-cerebras:latest"

# Update Edge TTS
TTS_ID=$(echo "$PROVIDERS" | jq -r '.data[] | select(.name == "Edge TTS (FREE)") | .id')
curl -s -X PATCH "http://localhost:3000/providers/$TTS_ID" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d "{
    \"config\": {
      \"image\": \"${REGISTRY_IP}:5000/avr-tts-edge:latest\",
      \"env\": {
        \"VOICE\": \"en-US-AvaMultilingualNeural\",
        \"RATE\": \"+10%\",
        \"PITCH\": \"+2Hz\"
      }
    }
  }" > /dev/null
echo "✅ Edge TTS updated to ${REGISTRY_IP}:5000/avr-tts-edge:latest"

echo ""
echo "✅ All providers updated with registry IP!"
echo ""

# Also add to Docker daemon config for insecure registries
echo "📝 Updating Docker daemon config..."
echo "0000" | sudo -S tee /etc/docker/daemon.json > /dev/null << DOCKER_EOF
{
  "insecure-registries": ["${REGISTRY_IP}:5000", "localhost:5000", "registry:5000"]
}
DOCKER_EOF

echo "0000" | sudo -S systemctl restart docker
sleep 3

# Restart AVR services
cd /home/user/Desktop/avr-app
docker compose restart

echo ""
echo "✅ Setup complete!"
echo ""
echo "Provider images:"
curl -s "http://localhost:3000/providers" -H "Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN" \
  | jq -r '.data[] | select(.config.image != null) | "  - \(.name): \(.config.image)"'
EOF
